<script type=""text/javascript""><![CDATA[fs._server.fire(""profile_v2_megaphone_marquee"",{event:""before"",type:""html""});]]></script><script type=""text/javascript""><![CDATA[fs._server.fire(""profile_v2_megaphone_marquee"",{event:""after"",type:""html""});]]></script><script type=""text/javascript""><![CDATA[fs._server.fire(""profile_v2_background"",{event:""before"",type:""html""});]]></script><div id=""background"" class=""profile-background""><h2>Background</h2><div class=""background-content ""><div id=""background-summary-container"" class=""background-section "" data-li-template=""summary_section""><div id=""background-summary"" class=""background-summary edit-default""><div class=""summary-header""><h3>Summary</h3></div><div id=""summary-item"" class=""editable-item section-item""><div id=""summary-item-view""><div class=""summary""><p class=""description"" dir=""ltr"">Civil society network and capacity development. Strategising and designing advocacy, mobilisation &amp; campaign initiatives through civil society engagement at local, national and regional level. Managing Government relations. Campaign and mobilisation<br/><br/>
Rights based approaches to Education, Disaster Risk Reduction (DRR), Resilience &amp; Climate Extremes, Social Protection, Child Rights, Early Childhood Programmes, Social Inclusion, Women Rights and Gender, Governance, Livelihood &amp; Food Rights.<br/><br/>
Conceptual, analytical and practical proficiency on designing, strategising, managing, implementing &amp; reviewing development programmes especially with civil society engagement &amp; targeting the poor and the marginalised people.<br/><br/>
Technical skills include Coalition Building and Capacity Development, Policy Research, Analysis and Review, Action Research; Public Finance, Budget Work/ Participatory Budget Analysis, Official Development Assistance (ODA), Public Private Partnership and Privatisation, Social / Community Audit, Logical Framework Analysis; Participatory tools and modules (PVA, PRA); Advocacy and Communication tools.<br/><br/>
Designed, led and contributed to numerous policy advocacy and campaigns initiatives i.e. Flexible School Calendar; Remote School Registration Programme; Mid-day School Meal; Mainstreaming Early Childhood Education Curriculum &amp; Manual; Ensuring rights of Children with Disability &amp; Indigenous children; Disaster resilient school curriculum &amp; infrastructural design; advocacy for education as a fundamental right &amp; Increasing National Education Budget.<br/><br/>
Experienced in working with DfID, Danida, ActionAid, NETZ, Save the Children and other National, International NGOs and Research Organisations in different capacities.<br/><br/>
Countries of Work Experience: Myanmar, Bangladesh, India, Nepal, Pakistan, Sri Lanka, Indonesia, Philippines, Malawi, Ghana and Uganda.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div id=""background-experience-container"" class=""background-section"" data-li-template=""experience_section""><div id=""background-experience"" class=""background-experience edit-default ""><h3>Experience</h3><div id=""experience-526230103"" class=""editable-item section-item current-position""><div id=""experience-526230103-view""><header><h5 class=""experience-logo"" aria-hidden=""true""><a href=""/company/15887?trk=prof-exp-company-name""><span data-tracking=""mcp_profile_sum"" class=""new-miniprofile-container /biz/miniprofile/15887?pathWildcard=15887"" data-li-url=""/biz/miniprofile/15887?pathWildcard=15887"" data-li-getjs=""https://static.licdn.com/scds/concat/common/js?h=40vfeoewuurexnhvi1o2qiknu&amp;fc=2""><strong><img class=""lazy-load"" src=""https://static.licdn.com/scds/common/u/img/spacer.gif"" data-li-src=""https://media.licdn.com/media/p/1/000/01c/06e/2e5f7b1.png"" alt=""""/></strong></span></a></h5><h4><a href=""https://www.linkedin.com/title/education-governance-adviser-%26-braced-project-manager?trk=mprofile_title"" title=""Learn more about this title"">Education Governance Adviser &amp; BRACED Project Manager</a></h4><h5><span data-tracking=""mcp_profile_sum"" class=""new-miniprofile-container /biz/miniprofile/15887?pathWildcard=15887"" data-li-url=""/biz/miniprofile/15887?pathWildcard=15887"" data-li-getjs=""https://static.licdn.com/scds/concat/common/js?h=40vfeoewuurexnhvi1o2qiknu&amp;fc=2""><strong><a href=""/company/15887?trk=prof-exp-company-name"" dir=""auto"">ActionAid</a></strong></span></h5></header><span class=""experience-date-locale""><time>March 2014</time> – Present (2 years 7 months)<span class=""locality"">Yangon, Myanmar</span></span><p class=""description summary-field-show-more"" dir=""ltr"">• Thematically lead ActionAid Myanmar’s (AAM) Education Programmes. • Provide technical, management &amp; advisory support to the Right to Education (RTE); Education Financing; &amp; Disaster Risk Reduction &amp; Climate Resilience (DRR&amp;CR) programmes of AAM. i.e.<br/>
o ECHO funded DIPECHO Project &amp; managed the Myanmar Consortium for Community Resilience (MCCR)<br/>

Contributing to the National Level Policy Development processes in these areas. i.e. actively engaged in the first Myanmar National Social Protection Strategic Plan development processes. <br/>
• Design &amp; introduce innovative rights based programmes involving community participation, capacity development; responsive governance &amp; financing. <br/>
o Education Book development <br/>
o Introducing proper monitoring practices for ensuring effective education service delivery<br/>
o Climate Resilient active Student group formation and action implementation<br/>

o Community Auditing as an Education intervention<br/>
• Develop the capacity of AAM staffs &amp; members of CSOs on RTE, DRR&amp;CR Assessment and Education Financing.<br/>
• Raise funds through introducing innovative concepts.</p></div></div><div id=""experience-183618219"" class=""editable-item section-item past-position""><div id=""experience-183618219-view""><header><h4><a href=""https://www.linkedin.com/title/capacity-development-adviser%2C-south-asia?trk=mprofile_title"" title=""Learn more about this title"">Capacity Development Adviser, South Asia</a></h4><h5><a href=""/vsearch/p?company=Asia+South+Pacific+Association+for+Basic+and+Adult+Education+%28ASPBAE%29&amp;trk=prof-exp-company-name"" name=""company"" title=""Find others who have worked at this company"" dir=""auto"">Asia South Pacific Association for Basic and Adult Education (ASPBAE)</a></h5></header><span class=""experience-date-locale""><time>September 2009</time> – <time>March 2014</time> (4 years 7 months)<span class=""locality"">South Asia</span></span><p class=""description summary-field-show-more"" dir=""ltr"">• Manage the Civil Society Education Fund (CSEF) project in South Asia which is implemented by the National Education Coalitions (NEC) of five countries i.e. Bangladesh, India, Pakistan, Nepal, &amp; Sri Lanka. <br/>

Developing Country Education Strategy. <br/>
